2020/05/04
FKを参照したTPC-H02の自然結合結果
PART.Where(
    PART=>((PART.P_SIZE==15) AndAlso new Regex(".*BRASS",Compiled).IsMatch(PART.P_TYPE))
).SelectMany(
    PART=>PART.FK_PARTSUPP_PART().Where(
        PARTSUPP=>(
            new <>f__AnonymousType2`2(
                <>h__TransparentIdentifier1=new <>f__AnonymousType1`2(
                    <>h__TransparentIdentifier0=<>h__TransparentIdentifier0,SUPPLIER=PARTSUPP.FK_PARTSUPP_SUPPLIER()
                ),
                NATION=new <>f__AnonymousType1`2(
                    <>h__TransparentIdentifier0=<>h__TransparentIdentifier0,SUPPLIER=PARTSUPP.FK_PARTSUPP_SUPPLIER()
                ).
                SUPPLIER.FK_SUPPLIER_NATION()).NATION.FK_NATION_REGION().R_NAME=="EUROPE"
            )
        ),
        (PART,PARTSUPP)=>new <>f__AnonymousType0`2(PART=PART,PARTSUPP=PARTSUPP)
    ).Select(
        <>h__TransparentIdentifier0=>new <>f__AnonymousType4`8(
            S_ACCTBAL=new <>f__AnonymousType3`2(
                <>h__TransparentIdentifier2=new <>f__AnonymousType2`2(

2020/05/20
02がすごく遅かったそのクエリはサブクエリ除いたら。終わることはない。
from PART in this.dbo.PART
join PARTSUPP in this.dbo.PARTSUPP on PART.P_PARTKEY equals PARTSUPP.PS_PARTKEY
join SUPPLIER in this.dbo.SUPPLIER on PARTSUPP.PS_SUPPKEY equals SUPPLIER.S_SUPPKEY
join NATION in this.dbo.NATION on SUPPLIER.S_NATIONKEY equals NATION.N_NATIONKEY
join REGION in this.dbo.REGION on NATION.N_REGIONKEY equals REGION.R_REGIONKEY
where
    PART.P_SIZE==35&&
    new Regex(".*BRASS",RegexOptions.Compiled).IsMatch(PART.P_TYPE)&&
    REGION.R_NAME=="EUROPE"&&
50秒で終了したのは順番を入れ替えて
from REGION in this.dbo.REGION
join NATION in this.dbo.NATION on REGION.R_REGIONKEY equals NATION.N_NATIONKEY
join SUPPLIER in this.dbo.SUPPLIER on NATION.N_NATIONKEY equals SUPPLIER.S_NATIONKEY
join PARTSUPP in this.dbo.PARTSUPP on SUPPLIER.S_SUPPKEY equals PARTSUPP.PS_SUPPKEY
join PART in this.dbo.PART on PARTSUPP.PS_PARTKEY equals PART.P_PARTKEY
where
    PART.P_SIZE==35&&
    new Regex(".*BRASS",RegexOptions.Compiled).IsMatch(PART.P_TYPE)&&
    REGION.R_NAME=="EUROPE"&&

Frontend
    ConnectAsync_CompletedはReceiveAsync,SendAsyncを起動する
    ReceiveAsync_Completedで==0の時は再接続を試みるために
        ReceiveSend_ManualResetEvent.WaitAll、FindAsync
    DiscoveryClient_FindCompletedでConnectAsyncに失敗したらFindAsync

tpc-c 5分
    let a=1
    a
{() => (a => a).Invoke(1)}
{() => 1}

    let b=2
    let a=1
    a+b
{() => (b => (a => (a + b)).Invoke(1)).Invoke(2)}
() => {
    (a => (a + 2)).Invoke(1)
}
() => {
    1 + 2
}

    let c=3
    let b=2
    let a=1
    a+b+c

    (
        c => {
            (
                b => {

                                (a + b) +

                }

    ).Invoke(3)

    )
}
